GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::onResetStream(Http::StreamResetReason,\n   242→                                                                        absl::string_view) {\n   243→  const bool expected_reset = expect_reset_;\n   244→  const bool goaway = received_no_error_goaway_;\n   245→  resetState();\n   246→\n   247→  if (expected_reset) {\n   248→    // Stream reset 272→    Http::GoAwayErrorCode error_code) {\n   273→  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"connection going away health_flags={}\", *client_,\n   274→                 HostUtility::healthFlagsToString(*host_));\n   275→  // If we have an active health check probe and receive a GOAWAY indicating\n   276→  // graceful shutdown, allow the probe to complete before closing the connection.\n   277→  // The connection request_encoder_->getStream().resetStream(Http::StreamResetReason::LocalReset);\n   292→    }\n   293→  }\n   294→  // client_ can already be destroyed if the host was removed during the failure callback above.\n   295→  if (client_ != nullptr) {\n   296→    client_->close(Network::ConnectionCloseType::Abort);\n   297→  }\n   298→}\n   299→\n   300→bool GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::isHealthCheckSucceeded(\n   301→    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status) const {\n   302→  if (grpc_status != Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Ok) {\n   303→    return false;\n   304→  }\n   305→\n   306→  if (!health_check_response_ ||\n   307→      health_check_response_->status() != grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckResponse::SERVING) {\n   308→    return false;\n   309→  }\n   310→\n   311→  return true;\n   312→}\n   313→\n   314→void GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::onRpcComplete(\n   315→    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status, const std::string& grpc_message, bool end_stream) {\n   316→  logHealthCheckStatus(grpc_status, grpc_message);\n   317→  if (isHealthCheckSucceeded(grpc_status)) {\n   318→    handleSuccess(false);\n   319→  } else {\n   320→    handleFailure(envoy::data::core::v3::ACTIVE);\n   321→  }\n   322→\n   323→  // Read the value as we may call resetState() and clear it.\n   324→  const bool goaway = received_no_error_goaway_;\n   325→\n   326→  // |end_stream| will be false if we decided to stop healthcheck before HTTP stream has ended -\n   327→  // invalid gRPC payload, unexpected message stream or wrong content-type.\n   328→  if (end_stream) {\n   329→    resetState();\n   330→  } else {\n   331→    // request_encoder_ can already be destroyed if the host was removed during the failure callback\n   332→    // above.\n   333→    if (request_encoder_ != nullptr) {\n   334→      // resetState() will be called by onResetStream().\n   335→      expect_reset_ = true;\n   336→      request_encoder_->getStream().resetStream(Http::StreamResetReason::LocalReset);\n   337→    }\n   338→  }\n   339→\n   340→  // client_ can already be destroyed if the host was removed during the failure callback above.\n   341→  if (client_ != nullptr && (!parent_.reuse_connection_ || goaway)) {\n   342→    client_->close(Network::ConnectionCloseType::Abort);\n   343→  }\n   344→}\n   345→\n resetState();\n\n  if (expected_reset) {\n    // Stream reset was initiated by us (bogus gRPC response, timeout or cluster host is going\n    // away). (client_ != nullptr) {\n    client_->close(Network::ConnectionCloseType::Abort);\n  }\n}\n\nbool GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::isHealthCheckSucceeded(\n    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status) const {\n  if (grpc_status != Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Ok) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  if (!health_check_response_ ||\n      health_check_response_->status() != grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckResponse::SERVING) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\nvoid GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::onRpcComplete(\n    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status, const std::string& grpc_message, bool end_stream) {\n  logHealthCheckStatus(grpc_status, grpc_message);\n  if (isHealthCheckSucceeded(grpc_status)) {\n    handleSuccess(false);\n  } else {\n    handleFailure(envoy::data::core::v3::ACTIVE);\n  }\n\n  // Read the value as we may call resetState() and clear it.\n  const bool goaway = received_no_error_goaway_;\n\n  // |end_stream| will be false if we decided to stop healthcheck before HTTP stream has ended -\n  // invalid gRPC client_->close(Network::ConnectionCloseType::Abort);\n  } else {\n    request_encoder_->getStream().resetStream(Http::StreamResetReason::LocalReset);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid GrpcHealthCheckerImpl::GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession::logHealthCheckStatus(\n    Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus grpc_status, const std::string& grpc_message) {\n  const char* service_status;\n  if
